{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01MubvtvTZDYqBAc4dYRX3N1","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01WpF9GGdias1m82FrRtXjWh","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/sessions/projects/-workspace/memory/MEMORY.md","content":"# Flipt OCI Storage with AWS ECR Auto-Refresh Implementation\n\n## Overview\nImplemented dynamic AWS ECR authentication for OCI bundles with automatic credential refresh capability via AWS credentials chain.\n\n## Problem Solved\n- **Issue**: Flipt configured with OCI storage couldn't continuously pull bundles from AWS ECR when using temporary credentials\n- **Root Cause**: Only static username/password authentication was supported; AWS ECR tokens expire (~12h) and pulls would fail after expiry\n- **Solution**: Implemented credential caching with automatic refresh based on token expiry time\n\n## Key Changes\n\n### 1. ECR Credential Refresh (`internal/oci/ecr/ecr.go`)\n- Added `credentialCache` struct to store credentials with expiry time\n- Added `sync.Mutex` for thread-safe credential access\n- Modified `Credential()` method to:\n  - Check if cached credentials are still valid\n  - Fetch fresh credentials if expired or not cached\n  - Cache new credentials with expiry time\n- Updated `fetchCredential()` to return `(auth.Credential, time.Time, error)`\n- Respects `ExpiresAt` from AWS ECR response, defaults to 12 hours if not provided\n\n### 2. Configuration Support\n- Existing `AuthenticationTypeAWSECR` constant already in place\n- `WithAWSECRCredentials()` function already implemented\n- Configuration validation already supports both `static` and `aws-ecr` auth types\n\n## How It Works\n\n### Credential Lifecycle\n1. First request for ECR repository triggers `Credential()` method\n2. AWS credentials chain loads (env vars, IAM role, etc.)\n3. ECR token fetched via `GetAuthorizationToken()`\n4. Credentials cached with expiry time from AWS response\n5. Subsequent requests within expiry window use cached credentials\n6. Expired credentials automatically refreshed on next request\n\n### AWS Credentials Chain\nThe implementation uses `config.LoadDefaultConfig()` which automatically:\n- Checks `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`/`AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` environment variables\n- Falls back to IAM role credentials (EC2 IMDS, Lambda execution role, etc.)\n- Supports AWS CLI credentials file\n- Works with assume-role configurations\n\n## Testing\n- All existing OCI tests pass\n- Added new test cases for credential expiry handling\n- Validates credentials with explicit `ExpiresAt` timestamp\n- Validates default 12-hour expiry when not provided\n- Tests for proper error handling\n\n## Configuration Example\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: 123456789.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/my-flags:latest\n    authentication:\n      type: aws-ecr\n    bundles_directory: /data/bundles\n    poll_interval: 30s\n```\n\n## Architecture Notes\n- Credentials are validated on each call but cached efficiently\n- Thread-safe with mutex protection\n- Works with all AWS credential providers (env, IAM roles, STS, etc.)\n- No external configuration needed beyond setting `authentication.type: aws-ecr`\n- Automatic refresh happens transparently to callers\n\n## Integration Points\n- Used in `internal/storage/fs/store/store.go` when configuring OCI storage\n- Called from `cmd/flipt/bundle.go` for bundle operations\n- Called from polling mechanism in `internal/storage/fs/oci/store.go`\n\n## Tested Scenarios\n✅ All OCI tests pass\n✅ Storage tests ECR Credential Refresh (`internal/oci/ecr/ecr.go`)\n- Added `credentialCache` struct to store credentials with expiry time\n- Added `sync.Mutex` for thread-safe credential access\n- Modified `Credential()` method to:\n  - Check if cached credentials are still valid\n  - Fetch fresh credentials if expired or not cached\n  - Cache new credentials with expiry time\n- Updated `fetchCredential()` to return `(auth.Credential, time.Time, error)`\n- Respects `ExpiresAt` from AWS ECR response, defaults to 12 hours if not provided\n\n### 2. Configuration Support\n- Existing `AuthenticationTypeAWSECR` constant already in place\n- `WithAWSECRCredentials()` function already implemented\n- Configuration validation already supports both `static` and `aws-ecr` auth types\n\n## How It Works\n\n### Credential Lifecycle\n1. First request for ECR repository triggers `Credential()` method\n2. AWS credentials chain loads (env vars, IAM role, etc.)\n3. ECR token fetched via `GetAuthorizationToken()`\n4. Credentials cached with expiry time from AWS response\n5. Subsequent requests within expiry window use cached credentials\n6. Expired credentials automatically refreshed on next request\n\n### AWS Credentials Chain\nThe implementation uses `config.LoadDefaultConfig()` which automatically:\n- Checks `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`/`AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` environment variables\n- Falls back to IAM role credentials (EC2 IMDS, Lambda execution role, etc.)\n- Supports AWS CLI credentials file\n- Works with assume-role configurations\n\n## Testing\n- All existing OCI tests pass\n- Added new test cases for credential expiry handling\n- Validates credentials with explicit `ExpiresAt` timestamp\n- Validates default 12-hour expiry when not provided\n- Tests for proper error handling\n\n## Configuration Example\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: 123456789.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/my-flags:latest\n    authentication:\n      type: aws-ecr\n    bundles_directory: /data/bundles\n    poll_interval: 30s\n```\n\n## Architecture Notes\n- Credentials are validated on each call but cached efficiently\n- Thread-safe with mutex protection\n- Works with all AWS credential providers (env, IAM roles, STS, etc.)\n- No external configuration needed beyond setting `authentication.type: aws-ecr`\n- Automatic refresh happens transparently to callers\n\n## Integration Points\n- Used in `internal/storage/fs/store/store.go` when configuring OCI storage\n- Called from `cmd/flipt/bundle.go` for bundle operations\n- Called from polling mechanism in `internal/storage/fs/oci/store.go`\n\n## Tested Scenarios\n✅ All OCI tests pass\n✅ Storage tests pass\n✅ ECR credential tests pass\n✅ Credential caching tests pass\n✅ Credential refresh on expiry tests pass\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
